Evita - Bremen 18/12/04

*Where to start with this? The video is really nice quality aside from occasional washout. Unfortunately a small chunk is skipped every time a scene changes or song ends, has to be deliberate but I can't imagine why and it's pretty frustrating. The production is quite odd, there are a few scenes that appear to have been invented from nowhere, and a bizarre sort of dance/wandering around section at the beginning which seems to go on forever with no actual point. A strange highlight was a sort of reverse 'defying gravity' effect during DCFMA with Eva in a gigantic dress towering above everyone. Ethan's not bad but Anna Maria is completely miscast vocally, she sounds as if she should be singing opera.*

Jesus Christ Superstar - Halle 03/04/04
Chris Murray, Stefan Vinzberg, Ines-Agnes Krautwurst, Olaf Schöder, Ki-Hyun Park, Robert Bily, Jordi Molina, Randy Diamond
*Some washout, generation loss and not many close ups. You can still follow the action however, as it's mostly a full stage shot. The camera's clearly on a tripod and the close ups that are there seem to be faded into rather than zoomed. Chris as a tattoed rockstar style Jesus does a great job, though I don't much like the Judas. It's an odd production, with a few different arrangements and act 1 ending after Gethsemane. Whoever did the lighting should be shot - this is the worst use of spotlights I've ever seen, and cutting off Jesus' head with a misplaced spotlight during most of Gethsemane is just unforgiveable. Performed in German.*

Miss Saigon - Making of Manila production
Fairly long documentary on the Manila production. Features the principles (Lea Salonga, Will Chase, Leo Valdez, Robert Sena, Ronn Smith, Lisa Capps, Isay Alvarez) - as well as the alternates (Cezarah Campos, Ima Castro, Jon Jon Briones, etc.) and has loads of interviews, audition footage, backstage stuff, etc. Also has various ensemble members (Miriam Valmores-Marasigan, Analin Bantug, etc.) presenting and singing bits from the show.
*Pretty rare, only trading this for something I desperately want.*

Miss Saigon - Manila 2000
Lea Salonga, Will Chase, Leo Valdez, Robert Sena, Ronn Smith, Lisa Capps, Isay Alvarez, Natalie Everett
*Pro-shot with lots of close ups. Not the distorted, incomplete version that circulates, this copy is beautiful and complete.*

Miss Saigon - US Tour, Chicago 2000
Mika Nishida, Will Swenson?, Orville Mendosa*?, Eugene Barry-Hill, Christine Alloca, Johnny Fernandez?, Adrienne Sam?
*Same video as the US Tour 1997 one (which is just a terribly low quality version of this already not great video) and the Chicago 16/07/00 one. All three are being traded as different videos, but I've done a comparison and they're all the same thing. This video has been mislabelled so often it's ridiculous and there's no way of being sure what the correct date or cast is, but I'd say 2000 is more likely than 1997 and it's probably from Chicago since two out of three versions have been labelled that way. This is often labelled as having Dina Lynne Morishita, Michelle Nigalan or Kristine Remigio but I'm certain it's Mika. I'm also pretty sure of Eugene & Christine but the others are the most likely guesses. Although these videos are usually labelled as having Joseph as the Engineer it's not him, I'm just not sure who it is.... my best guess would be Orville.*

Miss Saigon - Tuscon, US Tour 02/12/00
Cast unconfirmed but the Kim is Mika Nishida, Engineer is Joseph Anthony Foronda, and John is Eugene Barry-Hill. I'd guess Ellen is Christine Alloca and Chris is Will Swenson.

Miss Saigon - Plays in the Park, NJ Summer 2005
Voltaire Balderama, Emerita Alcid, Loren Christopher, Timothy Walton, Sarah Pettorsson, Anthony Ong, Keli B. Reagan, Frank Andrews, Yui Anzai, Megan Bussiere, Samantha Hahn
*Pro-shot. A wonderful production, mostly faithful to or influenced by the original staging. A lot of these type of productions tend to be just okay at best but I love this - this is how Miss Saigon should be done. Emerita is surprisingly wonderful as Kim considering her Gigi was so mediocre.*

Miss Saigon - Fullerton Civic Light Opera, Fullerton, CA 16/09/05
Kristine Remigio, Franc-Anton Harwart, Blake Pullen, Bonifacio Deoso Jr., Kelly Lamont, Mace Oliver
*Pro-shot. Staging follows the original as closely as it can considering obvious budget restraints, but mostly it's pretty impressive. I do wish someone had told the bar girls they were supposed to be from Vietnam not New York though, the accents did give me fits. Considering Kristine's been playing Kim for at least 8 years I was hoping for so much more from her - she sings it well but her acting is far too passive and lacking in passion or emotion. Blake is a dreadful actor and obviously fell straight off the all-American factory line, he has the oddest way of singing (in tune would help), but his voice does improve in act 2. Franc-Anton's alright, but Bonifacio and Mace completely outshine everyone else acting-wise. Kelly's very... pink.*

Romeo & Julia - Budapest 2004

*Pro-shot, not as clear and close as the commerically released Budapest pro-shot however, though does have some nice shots and sometimes gets angles the other doesn't. It's pretty clear why Sandor & Andrea were the understudies, they're both fairly unconvincing and unmemorable... Sandor dances well but his singing and acting don't come even close to Attila's in the role and he tends to look confused. Andrea's still doing her possessed demon thing. Excellent performances from Szilveszter, Zoltan & Arpad however...*

Romeo & Juliet - Moscow 23/10/05

*Pro-shot but quite shaky in places and dark. The camera switches views so quickly and frequently in places I started to get motion sickness. I assume it's the closing night due to extended curtain call, flowers, speeches, etc. Eduard reminds me a lot of Damien as Romeo and I loved Evgeniya, she's probably my favourite Juliet since she manages to be sweet but never overdoes it, has actual personality, and sings it beautifully without sounding like an out of breath child (Marjan, Cecilia, Jasmina - take note).*
